### [102] [AI Planning Framework for LLM-Based Web Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12710)
*Orit Shahnovsky,Rotem Dror*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文将Web任务建模为序列决策过程，建立了现代LLM智能体架构与传统规划范式的映射关系，提出了5个新的评估指标和794条人工标注轨迹数据集，用于诊断和评估智能体行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM智能体在处理Web任务时如同黑盒，难以诊断其失败原因或理解其规划过程，缺乏系统的分析框架来评估智能体的轨迹质量。

Method: 1. 将Web任务形式化为序列决策过程；2. 建立智能体架构到传统规划范式的映射分类法：Step-by-Step智能体对应广度优先搜索(BFS)，Tree Search智能体对应最佳优先树搜索，Full-Plan-in-Advance智能体对应深度优先搜索(DFS)；3. 提出5个新的评估指标来评估轨迹质量；4. 构建包含794条人工标注轨迹的WebArena基准数据集。

Result: 对比基线Step-by-Step智能体与新型Full-Plan-in-Advance智能体发现：Step-by-Step智能体与人类黄金轨迹对齐度更高（总体成功率38%），而Full-Plan-in-Advance智能体在元素准确性等技术指标上表现更优（89%）。

Conclusion: 不同的智能体架构在不同评估维度上各有优势，需要根据具体应用约束选择合适的架构，证明了所提出的评估指标体系对于智能体架构选择的重要性。

Abstract: Developing autonomous agents for web-based tasks is a core challenge in AI. While Large Language Model (LLM) agents can interpret complex user requests, they often operate as black boxes, making it difficult to diagnose why they fail or how they plan. This paper addresses this gap by formally treating web tasks as sequential decision-making processes. We introduce a taxonomy that maps modern agent architectures to traditional planning paradigms: Step-by-Step agents to Breadth-First Search (BFS), Tree Search agents to Best-First Tree Search, and Full-Plan-in-Advance agents to Depth-First Search (DFS). This framework allows for a principled diagnosis of system failures like context drift and incoherent task decomposition. To evaluate these behaviors, we propose five novel evaluation metrics that assess trajectory quality beyond simple success rates. We support this analysis with a new dataset of 794 human-labeled trajectories from the WebArena benchmark. Finally, we validate our evaluation framework by comparing a baseline Step-by-Step agent against a novel Full-Plan-in-Advance implementation. Our results reveal that while the Step-by-Step agent aligns more closely with human gold trajectories (38% overall success), the Full-Plan-in-Advance agent excels in technical measures such as element accuracy (89%), demonstrating the necessity of our proposed metrics for selecting appropriate agent architectures based on specific application constraints.

</details>


### [103] [On Using Machine Learning to Early Detect Catastrophic Failures in Marine Diesel Engines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12733)
*Francesco Maione,Paolo Lino,Giuseppe Giannino,Guido Maione*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于传感器偏差导数的早期检测方法，用于预测船舶发动机的灾难性故障，能够在传统报警触发前提前预警，使操作人员有时间安全停机和改变航线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 船舶发动机的灾难性故障具有突发性和不可预测性，对航行、船员和乘客构成严重威胁。现有研究主要集中在部件的渐进退化建模，对突发异常现象关注有限，而早期检测是应对此类故障的唯一有效措施。

Method: 基于真实故障发动机数据，该方法计算传感器实际读数与期望值之间偏差的导数，而非传统的偏差值本身。采用随机森林算法（经测试为最优机器学习算法）进行预测，并使用基于深度学习的数据增强技术解决训练数据获取问题。

Result: 仿真结果证实该方法能够提前检测到灾难性故障的发生，在测量值达到临界阈值和传统报警触发之前发出预警，使操作人员能够及时关闭发动机、防止损坏并安全改变航线。真实数据验证进一步增强了方法的鲁棒性和实用性。

Conclusion: 所提出的方法通过监测偏差导数而非偏差值本身，能够更早地识别异常动态，为操作人员提供宝贵的预警时间，有效预防灾难性故障造成的损害和意外动力损失，具有实际应用价值。

Abstract: Catastrophic failures of marine engines imply severe loss of functionality and destroy or damage the systems irreversibly. Being sudden and often unpredictable events, they pose a severe threat to navigation, crew, and passengers. The abrupt nature makes early detection the only effective countermeasure. However, research has concentrated on modeling the gradual degradation of components, with limited attention to sudden and anomalous phenomena. This work proposes a new method for early detection of catastrophic failures. Based on real data from a failed engine, the approach evaluates the derivatives of the deviation between actual sensor readings and expected values of engine variables. Predictions are obtained by a Random Forest, which is the most suitable Machine Learning algorithm among the tested ones. Traditional methods focus on deviations of monitored signals, whereas the proposed approach employs the derivatives of the deviations to provide earlier indications of abnormal dynamics, and to alert that a rapid and dangerous event is breaking out within the system. The method allows the detection of anomalies before measurements reach critical thresholds and alarms are triggered, which is the common method in industry. Consequently, operators can be warned in advance and shut down the engine, then prevent damage and unexpected power loss. Moreover, they have the time to safely change the ship route and avoid potential obstacles. Simulation results conf irm the effectiveness of the proposed approach in anticipating occurrence of catastrophic failures. Validation on real-world data further reinforces the robustness and practical applicability of the method. It is worth noting that data acquisition to train the predictive algorithm is not a problem, since a Deep Learning-based data augmentation procedure is used.

</details>


### [104] [ToolTree: Efficient LLM Agent Tool Planning via Dual-Feedback Monte Carlo Tree Search and Bidirectional Pruning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12740)
*Shuo Yang,Soyeon Caren Han,Yihao Ding,Shuhe Wang,Eduard Hoy*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了ToolTree，一种受蒙特卡洛树搜索启发的工具规划新范式，通过双阶段LLM评估和双向剪枝机制解决现有方法缺乏前瞻性的问题，在多个基准测试上平均性能提升约10%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型（LLM）代理的工具规划方法主要采用贪婪、反应式的工具选择策略，缺乏前瞻性，未能考虑工具间的依赖关系，在处理复杂的多步骤任务时表现不佳。

Method: 提出ToolTree框架，采用受蒙特卡洛树搜索启发的规划范式。核心方法包括：（1）双阶段LLM评估机制；（2）双向剪枝机制，在工具执行前后对低潜力分支进行剪枝，从而在扩展的工具使用序列中做出明智、自适应的决策。

Result: 在4个基准测试上进行了开放集和封闭集工具规划任务的实证评估，结果表明ToolTree在保持最高效率的同时持续提升性能，与最先进的规划范式相比实现了约10%的平均性能提升。

Conclusion: ToolTree成功解决了现有工具规划方法缺乏前瞻性的问题，证明了蒙特卡洛树搜索启发的规划范式结合双向剪枝机制在LLM代理工具规划任务中的有效性和优越性。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) agents are increasingly applied to complex, multi-step tasks that require interaction with diverse external tools across various domains. However, current LLM agent tool planning methods typically rely on greedy, reactive tool selection strategies that lack foresight and fail to account for inter-tool dependencies. In this paper, we present ToolTree, a novel Monte Carlo tree search-inspired planning paradigm for tool planning. ToolTree explores possible tool usage trajectories using a dual-stage LLM evaluation and bidirectional pruning mechanism that enables the agent to make informed, adaptive decisions over extended tool-use sequences while pruning less promising branches before and after the tool execution. Empirical evaluations across both open-set and closed-set tool planning tasks on 4 benchmarks demonstrate that ToolTree consistently improves performance while keeping the highest efficiency, achieving an average gain of around 10\% compared to the state-of-the-art planning paradigm.

</details>


### [105] [AI Model Modulation with Logits Redistribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12755)
*Zihan Wang,Zhongkui Ma,Xinguo Feng,Zhiyang Mei,Ethan Ma,Derui Wang,Minhui Xue,Guangdong Bai*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了AIM，一种新型模型调制范式，通过logits重分配策略，在无需重训练的情况下实现单模型多样化行为，支持效用和焦点两种调制模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模模型为满足模型所有者和用户的多样化需求通常需要维护多个专用版本，这导致了效率低下的问题。现有方法缺乏一种统一机制来使单一模型能够动态适应不同质量要求和关注特征需求。

Method: 提出了AIM（模型调制范式），包含两个关键调制模式：效用调制（允许模型所有者动态控制输出质量）和焦点调制（使用户能精确控制模型关注的输入特征）。核心技术是基于logits序统计特性的logits重分配策略，该方法无需训练数据、无需重训练。通过联合概率分布建立了形式化理论基础以确保调节能力。

Result: 在图像分类、语义分割和文本生成等多个任务上验证了AIM的实用性和通用性，涵盖ResNet、SegFormer和Llama等多种主流架构。实验证明了AIM能够有效实现模型调制目标。

Conclusion: AIM成功实现了一种高效的模型调制方案，能够在单一模型上实现多样化行为，为模型所有者和用户提供了灵活的控制机制，具有广泛的应用前景。

Abstract: Large-scale models are typically adapted to meet the diverse requirements of model owners and users. However, maintaining multiple specialized versions of the model is inefficient. In response, we propose AIM, a novel model modulation paradigm that enables a single model to exhibit diverse behaviors to meet the specific end requirements. AIM enables two key modulation modes: utility and focus modulations. The former provides model owners with dynamic control over output quality to deliver varying utility levels, and the latter offers users precise control to shift model's focused input features. AIM introduces a logits redistribution strategy that operates in a training data-agnostic and retraining-free manner. We establish a formal foundation to ensure AIM's regulation capability, based on the statistical properties of logits ordering via joint probability distributions. Our evaluation confirms AIM's practicality and versatility for Al model modulation, with tasks spanning image classification, semantic segmentation and text generation, and prevalent architectures including ResNet, SegFormer and Llama.

</details>


### [106] [Context is all you need: Towards autonomous model-based process design using agentic AI in flowsheet simulations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12813)
*Pascal Schäfer,Lukas J. Krinke,Martin Wlotzka,Norbert Asprion*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个多智能体AI框架，用于辅助化工流程模拟环境中的建模工作。该框架结合先进的LLM（如Claude Opus 4.6）与推理能力，能够分解流程开发任务：一个智能体利用工程知识解决抽象问题，另一个智能体将其实现为Chemasim代码。在反应/分离过程、变压精馏和杂共沸精馏等典型案例中验证了框架的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

### [109] [Structured Distillation for Personalized Agent Memory: 11x Token Reduction with Retrieval Preservation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13017)
*Sydney Lewis*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种个性化AI代理记忆压缩方法，将对话历史蒸馏为紧凑的检索层，实现11倍压缩（平均每次交互从371个token降至38个），在保持96%检索质量（MRR）的同时，显著降低了上下文成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 与AI代理的长对话历史对用户有价值，但完整保留对话历史的成本过高。如何在压缩存储成本的同时，保留个性化记忆的检索能力，是亟待解决的问题。

Method: 提出结构化蒸馏方法，将每次交互压缩为包含四个字段（exchange_core、specific_context、thematic room_assignments、regex-extracted files_touched）的复合对象，平均生成38个token的可搜索文本。在4,182个对话（14,340次交互）上，使用201个召回查询、107种配置（涵盖5种纯检索和5种跨层检索模式）以及5个LLM评分器进行评估。

Result: 实现11倍压缩（371→38 tokens）。最佳纯蒸馏配置MRR达到0.717，为最佳原始基线（MRR 0.745）的96%。向量检索的20种配置在Bonferroni校正后均不显著，BM25的20种配置显著退化（效应量|d|=0.031-0.756）。最佳跨层配置MRR达0.759，略超最佳纯原始基线。

Conclusion: 结构化蒸馏能够在压缩单用户代理记忆至原成本1/11的同时，不牺牲检索质量，支持数千次交互放入单个提示，同时保留原始数据用于深度查询。

Abstract: Long conversations with an AI agent create a simple problem for one user: the history is useful, but carrying it verbatim is expensive. We study personalized agent memory: one user's conversation history with an agent, distilled into a compact retrieval layer for later search. Each exchange is compressed into a compound object with four fields (exchange_core, specific_context, thematic room_assignments, and regex-extracted files_touched). The searchable distilled text averages 38 tokens per exchange. Applied to 4,182 conversations (14,340 exchanges) from 6 software engineering projects, the method reduces average exchange length from 371 to 38 tokens, yielding 11x compression. We evaluate whether personalized recall survives that compression using 201 recall-oriented queries, 107 configurations spanning 5 pure and 5 cross-layer search modes, and 5 LLM graders (214,519 consensus-graded query-result pairs). The best pure distilled configuration reaches 96% of the best verbatim MRR (0.717 vs 0.745). Results are mechanism-dependent. All 20 vector search configurations remain non-significant after Bonferroni correction, while all 20 BM25 configurations degrade significantly (effect sizes |d|=0.031-0.756). The best cross-layer setup slightly exceeds the best pure verbatim baseline (MRR 0.759). Structured distillation compresses single-user agent memory without uniformly sacrificing retrieval quality. At 1/11 the context cost, thousands of exchanges fit within a single prompt while the verbatim source remains available for drill-down. We release the implementation and analysis pipeline as open-source software.

### [110] [Beyond Final Answers: CRYSTAL Benchmark for Transparent Multimodal Reasoning Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13099)
*Wayner Barrios,SouYoung Jin*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了CRYSTAL基准，通过可验证的中间步骤评估多模态推理能力，并提出CPR奖励机制，在训练中显著提升推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估方法仅关注最终答案准确性，无法发现模型在推理过程中的系统性问题，如步骤遗漏、顺序混乱等，因此需要一个新的诊断性基准来细粒度评估多模态推理的中间过程。

Method: 构建包含6,372个实例的CRYSTAL基准，采用Delphi启发式流程构建参考轨迹；提出Match F1和Ordered Match F1两个指标评估步骤级精确率、召回率和顺序正确性；设计Causal Process Reward (CPR)奖励函数，将答案正确性与步骤对齐相耦合，并提出CPR-Curriculum渐进式训练策略。

Result: 对20个MLLM（包括未参与基准构建的前沿商业系统）的评估揭示了普遍性问题：精确率远高于召回率（选择性 cherry-picking）、非单调的规模权衡、以及推理步骤顺序混乱（最优模型仅保留60%的正确顺序步骤）；CPR-Curriculum通过GRPO训练使Match F1提升32%，而传统加性奖励策略则无效。

Conclusion: CRYSTAL基准能够揭示传统准确率指标无法发现的推理缺陷；CPR-Curriculum训练方法无需人工步骤标注即可有效提升模型的多模态推理能力，为推理过程的质量提升提供了新方向。

Abstract: We introduce **CRYSTAL** (*__C__lear __R__easoning via __Y__ielded __S__teps, __T__raceability and __L__ogic*), a diagnostic benchmark with 6,372 instances that evaluates multimodal reasoning through verifiable intermediate steps. We propose two complementary metrics: *Match F1*, which scores step-level precision and recall via semantic similarity matching, and *Ordered Match F1*, which further penalizes disordered reasoning chains. References are constructed through a Delphi-inspired pipeline where four independent MLLMs generate trajectories, aggregated via semantic clustering and validated through human quality gates. Evaluation of 20 MLLMs, including commercial frontier systems not used during benchmark construction, reveals systematic failures invisible to accuracy: universal cherry-picking (precision far exceeds recall), non-monotonic scaling trade-offs, and disordered reasoning where no competitive model preserves more than 60% of matched steps in correct order. Beyond evaluation, we propose the **Causal Process Reward (CPR)**, a multiplicative reward that couples answer correctness with step-level alignment, and **CPR-Curriculum**, which progressively increases reasoning difficulty during training. CPR-Curriculum achieves +32% Match F1 via GRPO where additive reward strategies fail, improving reasoning without manual step annotation.

### [111] [Steve-Evolving: Open-World Embodied Self-Evolution via Fine-Grained Diagnosis and Dual-Track Knowledge Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13131)
*Zhengwei Xie,Zhisheng Chen,Ziyan Weng,Tingyu Wu,Chenglong Li,Vireo Zhang,Kun Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了Steve-Evolving框架，一种面向开放世界具身智能体的非参数自演化方法，通过闭环机制结合细粒度执行诊断与双轨知识蒸馏，有效解决长视野任务中的交互经验组织与演化问题，在Minecraft MCU基准测试上取得了显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开放世界具身智能体在解决长视野任务时，主要瓶颈不在于单步规划质量，而在于如何有效组织和演化交互经验。现有方法难以充分挖掘和利用执行过程中的细粒度诊断信息，且缺乏有效的经验组织机制。

Method: 提出Steve-Evolving非参数自演化框架，包含三个阶段：(1)经验锚定：将子目标尝试固化为结构化经验元组（前状态、动作、诊断结果、后状态），构建三层经验空间与多维索引；(2)经验蒸馏：成功轨迹泛化为可复用技能，失败轨迹蒸馏为可执行护栏；(3)知识驱动闭环控制：将技能与护栏注入LLM规划器，诊断触发的局部重规划在线更新约束，形成无需参数更新的持续演化过程。

Result: 在Minecraft MCU长视野任务基准测试上，该方法相比静态检索基线取得了持续且一致的性能提升，验证了细粒度诊断与双轨知识蒸馏闭环机制的有效性。

Conclusion: 通过紧密耦合细粒度执行诊断与双轨知识蒸馏的闭环机制，Steve-Evolving实现了交互经验的有效组织与持续演化，为开放世界具身智能体解决长视野任务提供了一种无需模型参数更新的新范式。

Abstract: Open-world embodied agents must solve long-horizon tasks where the main bottleneck is not single-step planning quality but how interaction experience is organized and evolved. To this end, we present Steve-Evolving, a non-parametric self-evolving framework that tightly couples fine-grained execution diagnosis with dual-track knowledge distillation in a closed loop. The method follows three phases: Experience Anchoring, Experience Distillation, and Knowledge-Driven Closed-Loop Control. In detail, Experience Anchoring solidifies each subgoal attempt into a structured experience tuple with a fixed schema (pre-state, action, diagnosis-result, and post-state) and organizes it in a three-tier experience space with multi-dimensional indices (e.g., condition signatures, spatial hashing, and semantic tags) plus rolling summarization for efficient and auditable recall. To ensure sufficient information density for attribution, the execution layer provides compositional diagnosis signals beyond binary outcomes, including state-difference summaries, enumerated failure causes, continuous indicators, and stagnation/loop detection. Moreover, successful trajectories of Experience Distillation are generalized into reusable skills with explicit preconditions and verification criteria, while failures are distilled into executable guardrails that capture root causes and forbid risky operations at both subgoal and task granularities. Besides, Knowledge-Driven Closed-Loop Control retrieved skills and guardrails are injected into an LLM planner, and diagnosis-triggered local replanning updates the active constraints online, forming a continual evolution process without any model parameter updates. Experiments on the long-horizon suite of Minecraft MCU demonstrate consistent improvements over static-retrieval baselines.

### [112] [When Right Meets Wrong: Bilateral Context Conditioning with Reward-Confidence Correction for GRPO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13134)
*Yu Li,Tian Lan,Zhengling Qi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出BICC和RCC两种改进机制，通过对比学习充分利用正确与错误样本间的差异信号，并动态调整优势基线以稳定训练，在无需额外采样或辅助模型的情况下显著提升了GRPO在数学推理任务上的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GRPO在计算优势时基于组均值，但在优化过程中将每个输出视为独立样本，忽略了组内正确与错误解法之间的自然对比结构信号，未充分利用成功与失败推理轨迹间的比较信息。

Method: 提出双上下文条件化(BICC)机制，使模型在优化过程中能够交叉引用成功和失败的推理轨迹；引入奖励置信度校正(RCC)，利用奖励-置信度协方差动态调整优势基线。两种机制无需额外采样或辅助模型，可适配所有GRPO变体。

Result: 在数学推理基准测试上的实验表明，该方法在多种模型和算法上均取得一致的改进效果。

Conclusion: 通过对比重构GRPO目标函数，显式利用正确与错误样本间的边界最大化，BICC和RCC机制有效增强了推理模型的训练效果，为GRPO系列方法提供了通用的改进方案。

Abstract: Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) has emerged as an effective method for training reasoning models. While it computes advantages based on group mean, GRPO treats each output as an independent sample during the optimization and overlooks a vital structural signal: the natural contrast between correct and incorrect solutions within the same group, thus ignoring the rich, comparative data that could be leveraged by explicitly pitting successful reasoning traces against failed ones. To capitalize on this, we present a contrastive reformulation of GRPO, showing that the GRPO objective implicitly maximizes the margin between the policy ratios of correct and incorrect samples. Building on this insight, we propose Bilateral Context Conditioning (BICC), a mechanism that allows the model to cross-reference successful and failed reasoning traces during the optimization, enabling a direct information flow across samples. We further introduce Reward-Confidence Correction (RCC) to stabilize training by dynamically adjusts the advantage baseline in GRPO using reward-confidence covariance derived from the first-order approximation of the variance-minimizing estimator. Both mechanisms require no additional sampling or auxiliary models and can be adapted to all GRPO variants. Experiments on mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate consistent improvements across comprehensive models and algorithms. Code is available at \href{https://github.com/Skylanding/BiCC}{https://github.com/Skylanding/BiCC}.

</details>


### [113] [Developing and evaluating a chatbot to support maternal health care](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13168)

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一个面向印度孕产妇健康的手机聊天机器人系统，通过结合分诊、检索和LLM生成，并提出了针对高风险场景的多元评估工作流，验证了在多语言、噪声环境下构建可信医疗助手需要纵深防御设计与多方法评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 系统结合三方面技术：(1)阶段感知分诊，将高风险查询路由至专家模板；(2)基于精选孕产妇/新生儿指南的混合检索；(3)基于证据条件的LLM生成。核心贡献是提出了有限专家监督下的高风险部署评估工作流，包括：标注分诊基准测试(N=150)、合成多证据检索基准测试(N=100)、基于临床医生协同标准的LLM-as-judge比较(N=781)，以及专家验证。

Conclusion: 在多语言、噪声环境下构建可信医疗助手需要纵深防御设计配合多方法评估，而非依赖单一模型和评估方法选择。

Abstract: The ability to provide trustworthy maternal health information using phone-based chatbots can have a significant impact, particularly in low-resource settings where users have low health literacy and limited access to care. However, deploying such systems is technically challenging: user queries are short, underspecified, and code-mixed across languages, answers require regional context-specific grounding, and partial or missing symptom context makes safe routing decisions difficult.
  We present a chatbot for maternal health in India developed through a partnership between academic researchers, a health tech company, a public health nonprofit, and a hospital. The system combines (1) stage-aware triage, routing high-risk queries to expert templates, (2) hybrid retrieval over curated maternal/newborn guidelines, and (3) evidence-conditioned generation from an LLM. Our core contribution is an evaluation workflow for high-stakes deployment under limited expert supervision. Targeting both component-level and end-to-end testing, we introduce: (i) a labeled triage benchmark (N=150) achieving 86.7% emergency recall, explicitly reporting the missed-emergency vs. over-escalation trade-off; (ii) a synthetic multi-evidence retrieval benchmark (N=100) with chunk-level evidence labels; (iii) LLM-as-judge comparison on real queries (N=781) using clinician-codesigned criteria; and (iv) expert validation. Our findings show that trustworthy medical assistants in multilingual, noisy settings require defense-in-depth design paired with multi-method evaluation, rather than any single model and evaluation method choice.

</details>


### [114] [Semantic Invariance in Agentic AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13173)
*I. de Zarzà,J. de Curtò,Jordi Cabot,Pietro Manzoni,Carlos T. Calafate*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个蜕变测试框架，用于系统评估LLM推理代理的语义不变性。通过对7个基础模型应用8种语义保持变换，发现模型规模并不预测鲁棒性：较小的Qwen3-30B-A3B实现了最高稳定性（79.6%不变响应），而更大的模型反而表现出更大的脆弱性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM越来越多地作为自主推理代理应用于决策支持、科学问题求解和多代理协调系统。然而，在这些关键应用中部署LLM代理需要确保其推理在语义等价的输入变化下保持稳定（即语义不变性）。现有的标准基准评估仅评估固定、规范问题表述上的准确性，无法捕捉这一关键可靠性维度。

Method: 提出了一个蜕变测试框架，系统评估LLM推理代理的鲁棒性。对7个基础模型（涵盖4个不同架构家族：Hermes 70B/405B、Qwen3 30B-A3B/235B-A22B、DeepSeek-R1、gpt-oss 20B/120B）应用8种语义保持变换（恒等、改写、事实重排序、扩展、收缩、学术语境、商业语境和对比表述），在8个科学领域的19个多步推理问题进行评估。

Result: 模型规模并不预测鲁棒性：较小的Qwen3-30B-A3B实现了最高稳定性（79.6%不变响应，语义相似度0.91），而更大的模型表现出更大的脆弱性。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了LLM推理代理在语义等价输入变化下的稳定性问题，证明了模型规模与鲁棒性之间不存在简单的正相关关系，为LLM在关键应用中的可靠部署提供了重要的评估方法和见解。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) increasingly serve as autonomous reasoning agents in decision support, scientific problem-solving, and multi-agent coordination systems. However, deploying LLM agents in consequential applications requires assurance that their reasoning remains stable under semantically equivalent input variations, a property we term semantic invariance.Standard benchmark evaluations, which assess accuracy on fixed, canonical problem formulations, fail to capture this critical reliability dimension. To address this shortcoming, in this paper we present a metamorphic testing framework for systematically assessing the robustness of LLM reasoning agents, applying eight semantic-preserving transformations (identity, paraphrase, fact reordering, expansion, contraction, academic context, business context, and contrastive formulation) across seven foundation models spanning four distinct architectural families: Hermes (70B, 405B), Qwen3 (30B-A3B, 235B-A22B), DeepSeek-R1, and gpt-oss (20B, 120B). Our evaluation encompasses 19 multi-step reasoning problems across eight scientific domains. The results reveal that model scale does not predict robustness: the smaller Qwen3-30B-A3B achieves the highest stability (79.6% invariant responses, semantic similarity 0.91), while larger models exhibit greater fragility.

</details>

Our analysis highlights that datacenter dynamics can influence their effectiveness and that combining strategies can significantly lower emissions, but introduces complex cost-emissions-performance trade-offs that STEAM can help navigate. STEAM supports the integration of new models and techniques, making it a foundation framework for holistic, quantitative, and reproducible research in sustainable computing. Following open-science principles, STEAM is available as FOSS: https://github.com/atlarge-research/OpenDC-STEAM.

### [117] [KernelFoundry: Hardware-aware evolutionary GPU kernel optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12440)
*Nina Wiedemann,Quentin Leboutet,Michael Paulitsch,Diana Wofk,Benjamin Ummenhofer*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了KernelFoundry，一个用于优化GPU内核的进化框架，通过MAP-Elites质量多样性搜索、元提示进化和模板参数优化三个机制，有效探索GPU内核设计空间，在KernelBench上实现平均2.3倍的加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于大语言模型的内核生成方法主要依赖简单提示和反馈循环，仅通过性能分析反馈间接引入硬件感知，难以有效处理LLM内核优化中涉及的硬件架构理解、并行优化策略和性能分析等复杂挑战。

Method: 提出KernelFoundry进化框架，包含三个关键机制：（1）基于MAP-Elites的质量多样性搜索，利用内核特定的行为维度维持跨多样化优化策略的探索；（2）元提示进化，与内核协同进化提示以发现任务特定的优化策略；（3）基于模板的参数优化，针对输入和硬件调整内核。该框架实现为分布式架构，支持远程访问多样化硬件。

Result: 在KernelBench、robust-kbench和自定义任务上进行评估，生成SYCL内核（跨平台GPU编程模型）和CUDA内核。该方法持续优于基线方法，在KernelBench上SYCL内核平均加速达2.3倍。

Conclusion: KernelFoundry作为一个分布式框架，通过远程访问多样化硬件实现快速基准测试，具有灵活的用户输入层，支持超越基准测试的广泛实际应用场景的内核生成，有效解决了GPU内核优化挑战。

Abstract: Optimizing GPU kernels presents a significantly greater challenge for large language models (LLMs) than standard code generation tasks, as it requires understanding hardware architecture, parallel optimization strategies, and performance profiling outputs. Most existing LLM-based approaches to kernel generation rely on simple prompting and feedback loops, incorporating hardware awareness only indirectly through profiling feedback. We introduce KernelFoundry, an evolutionary framework that efficiently explores the GPU kernel design space through three key mechanisms: (1) MAP-Elites quality-diversity search with kernel-specific behavioral dimensions to sustain exploration across diverse optimization strategies; (2) meta-prompt evolution, which co-evolves prompts with kernels to uncover task-specific optimization strategies, and (3) template-based parameter optimization to tune kernels to inputs and hardware. We evaluate this framework on KernelBench, robust-kbench, and custom tasks, generating SYCL kernels as a cross-platform GPU programming model and CUDA kernels for comparison to prior work. Our approach consistently outperforms the baseline methods, achieving an average speedup of 2.3x on KernelBench for SYCL. Moreover, KernelFoundry is implemented as a distributed framework with remote access to diverse hardware, enabling rapid benchmarking and featuring a flexible user input layer that supports kernel generation for a wide range of real-world use cases beyond benchmarking.

</details>


### [118] [TaxBreak: Unmasking the Hidden Costs of LLM Inference Through Overhead Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12465)
*Prabhu Vellaisamy,Shreesh Tripathi,Vignesh Natarajan,Surya Santhan Thenarasu,Shawn Blanton,John P. Shen*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 提出了TaxBreak方法，将大语言模型推理中的主机端编排开销分解为框架转换、CUDA库转换和内核启动路径三个组件，并引入主机-设备平衡指数(HDBI)来识别优化目标，发现MoE模型在主机受限场景下CPU单线程性能是影响端到端延迟的关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型推理在延迟敏感部署中，主机端开销可能成为主要瓶颈。现有方法仅暴露聚合残余或启动/队列指标，无法精确定位需要优化的执行层，缺乏对主机端编排开销的细粒度分解能力。

Method: 提出TaxBreak方法，将主机端编排开销分解为框架转换时间、CUDA库转换时间和内核启动路径时间三个组件；引入主机-设备平衡指数(HDBI)来关联设备活跃执行与主机可见编排；在NVIDIA H100和H200系统上验证该方法。

Result: MoE模型每个输出token调度8-11倍于稠密模型的内核数量；对于主机受限工作负载，CPU单线程性能是一阶参数：更快的CPU可减少10-29%的编排开销并改善高达14%的端到端延迟，即使搭配较慢时钟的GPU；聚合延迟、GPU不活动或有界比率单独使用会掩盖主要优化目标。

Conclusion: TaxBreak作为诊断工具可有效区分应优化软件栈开销还是设备端工作负载执行的场景，为优化决策提供了明确指导。

Abstract: Large Language Model (LLM) inference is widely used in interactive assistants and agentic systems. In latency-sensitive deployments, inference time can become dominated by host-side overheads. Existing approaches typically expose this cost only as an aggregate residual or a launch/queue metric, which is often insufficient to identify which execution layer should be optimized. This work presents TaxBreak, a trace-driven methodology for decomposing host-visible orchestration overhead into three components: framework translation time, CUDA library translation time, and kernel launch-path time. We validate TaxBreak on NVIDIA H100 and H200 systems and use it to derive our proposed Host-Device Balance Index (HDBI), a boundedness summary index that relates device-active execution to host-visible orchestration. Across representative dense and mixture-of-experts workloads in both prefill and decode, we show that aggregate latency, GPU inactivity, or boundedness ratios alone can obscure the dominant optimization target. TaxBreak instead distinguishes cases where optimization should reduce software-stack overhead from cases where the primary win comes from reducing device-side work. We further show that MoE models dispatch 8-11x more kernels per output token than dense models, and that for such host-bound workloads, CPU single-thread performance is a first-order parameter: a faster host CPU reduces orchestration overhead by 10-29% and improves end-to-end latency by up to 14%, even when paired with a slower-clocked GPU. These results position TaxBreak as a diagnostic tool for assessing whether optimization effort should target the software stack or the device-side workload execution.

</details>


### [119] [Streaming REST APIs for Large Financial Transaction Exports from Relational Databases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12566)
*Abhiram Kandiraju*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于流式传输的REST API架构，用于解决金融和企业管理系统中大规模交易数据导出时的内存消耗和响应延迟问题，实现了边处理边传输的高效数据导出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的REST API在处理大规模交易数据导出（数十万至数百万条记录）时，通常需要在内存中构建完整的导出负载后再传输，导致内存消耗过高且响应启动延迟，无法满足金融平台对报表、对账、审计和合规性检查的性能需求。

Method: 提出了一种流式REST API架构，将关系型数据库的游标检索与HTTP响应输出流的渐进式传输相结合。该架构使用Java JAX-RS框架和StreamingOutput接口实现，支持从数据库增量检索交易记录并直接写入HTTP响应流，无需在内存中组装完整数据集。支持CSV、OFX、QFX和QBO等多种金融导出格式。

Result: 流式传输方法显著降低了内存缓冲需求，允许大规模导出下载立即开始，无需等待完整数据集组装完成。该方法提高了高容量导出操作的响应速度和系统可扩展性，有效解决了传统方法在处理大数据集时的性能瓶颈。

Conclusion: 流式REST API架构为金融平台和企业系统的大规模交易数据导出提供了可行的技术解决方案，通过数据库游标与HTTP流传输的集成，在保证数据完整性的同时优化了资源使用效率，适用于对性能和可扩展性要求较高的生产环境。

Abstract: Financial platforms and enterprise systems frequently provide transaction export capabilities to support reporting, reconciliation, auditing, and regulatory compliance workflows. In many environments, these exports involve very large datasets containing hundreds of thousands or even millions of transaction records. Traditional REST API implementations often construct the entire export payload in application memory before transmitting the response to the client, which can lead to high memory consumption and delayed response initiation when processing large datasets. This paper presents a streaming-based REST API architecture that retrieves transaction records incrementally from relational databases and writes them directly to the HTTP response output stream. By integrating database cursor retrieval with progressive HTTP transmission, the proposed design allows export data to be delivered continuously as records are processed rather than after the full dataset has been assembled. The architecture is implemented using a Java-based JAX-RS framework with the StreamingOutput interface and supports multiple financial export formats including CSV, OFX, QFX, and QBO. In practice, the streaming approach significantly reduces memory buffering requirements and allows large export downloads to begin immediately, improving responsiveness and scalability for high-volume export operations.

</details>


### [120] [Serving Hybrid LLM Loads with SLO Guarantees Using CPU-GPU Attention Piggybacking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12831)
*Zizhao Mo,Junlin Chen,Huanle Xu,Chengzhong Xu*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了OmniServe系统，通过Attention Piggybacking机制将BE服务的注意力计算卸载到CPU，并采用动态批处理控制策略，在共享集群中同时提升了延迟敏感服务的SLO达成率和最佳努力服务的吞吐量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前共享集群中多类型LLM服务共存存在两大问题：(1)服务共存引入的干扰风险威胁延迟敏感(LS)服务的SLO合规性；(2)有限的可用内存严重制约了最佳努力(BE)服务的能力。现有系统依赖预留余量来约束BE资源使用，但粒度过粗，既损害LS服务的SLO合规性，又不必要地限制了BE服务的生成潜力。

Method: 提出OmniServe系统，核心创新包括：(1)Attention Piggybacking机制，动态将BE服务的注意力计算卸载到CPU；(2)异步CPU-GPU流通信，防止GPU在聚合注意力结果时被阻塞；(3)动态批处理控制策略，适应请求到达的波动，利用分层批处理促进Dense模块计算。

Result: 实验结果表明，与最先进的系统相比，OmniServe将LS服务的SLO达成率提升最高1.48倍，同时将BE服务吞吐量提升最高9.85倍。

Conclusion: OmniServe通过高效利用CPU和GPU资源协同计算，有效缓解了共享集群中服务间的干扰问题，在保障LS服务性能的同时显著提升了BE服务的吞吐量，为多类型LLM服务共存提供了高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Nowadays, service providers often deploy multiple types of LLM services within shared clusters. While the service colocation improves resource utilization, it introduces significant interference risks for latency-sensitive (LS) services-which have strict SLO requirements for inference latency-and severely constrain the service capacity of best-effort (BE) services due to limited available memory. To address interference, existing systems typically rely on reserving headroom to constrain BE resource usage. However, this approach's coarse granularity compromises the SLO compliance of the latency-sensitive service and unnecessarily restricts the generation potential of the best effort service.
  In this paper, we propose OmniServe, a novel LLM serving system that efficiently harnesses both CPU and GPU resources to mitigate interference and improve throughput. Central to OmniServe is the Attention Piggybacking mechanism, which effectively offloads the Attention computation of BE services to CPUs on the fly. This mechanism also facilitates asynchronous communication between CPU and GPU streams, preventing GPUs from being blocked while aggregating Attention results. Additionally, OmniServe incorporates a dynamic batching control policy to adapt to fluctuating request arrivals, facilitating Dense module computation using layer-wise batching. Experimental results show that OmniServe improves the SLO attainment rate for LS services by up to $1.48\times$ while enhancing BE serving throughput by up to $9.85\times$ compared to state-of-the-art systems.

</details>


### [121] [ARL-Tangram: Unleash the Resource Efficiency in Agentic Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13019)
*Bangjun Xiao,Yihao Zhao,Xiangwei Deng,Shihua Yu,Yuxing Xiang,Huaqiu Liu,Qiying Wang,Liang Zhao,Hailin Zhang,Xuanzhe Liu,Xin Jin,Fuli Luo*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出了ARL-Tangram系统，通过action级别的细粒度编排解决代理强化学习中外部云资源利用率低的问题，显著提升了任务完成速度并大幅节省资源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代理强化学习（Agentic RL）需要大量外部云资源（如CPU用于代码执行、GPU用于奖励模型），但现有框架采用静态过度配置策略，资源绑定到长期轨迹或按任务隔离，导致严重的资源低效问题。

Method: 提出action级别编排策略，构建统一的资源管理系统ARL-Tangram。系统采用统一的action级别形式化表示和弹性调度算法，在满足异构资源约束的前提下最小化动作完成时间（ACT）；针对异构资源特性与拓扑结构定制异构资源管理器以高效支持action级别执行。

Result: 在真实代理强化学习任务上的评估表明，ARL-Tangram将平均动作完成时间（ACT）提升最多4.3倍，RL训练步长速度提升最多1.5倍，外部资源节省最多71.2%。该系统已部署支持MiMo系列模型的训练。

Conclusion: action级别的细粒度资源编排与统一管理系统能够有效解决代理强化学习中的资源低效问题，显著提升训练效率并大幅降低资源消耗，已在实际生产环境中验证其有效性。

Abstract: Agentic reinforcement learning (RL) has emerged as a transformative workload in cloud clusters, enabling large language models (LLMs) to solve complex problems through interactions with real world. However, unlike traditional RL, agentic RL demands substantial external cloud resources, e.g., CPUs for code execution and GPUs for reward models, that exist outside the primary training cluster. Existing agentic RL framework typically rely on static over-provisioning, i.e., resources are often tied to long-lived trajectories or isolated by tasks, which leads to severe resource inefficiency.
  We propose the action-level orchestration, and incorporate it into ARL-Tangram, a unified resource management system that enables fine-grained external resource sharing and elasticity. ARL-Tangram utilizes a unified action-level formulation and an elastic scheduling algorithm to minimize action completion time (ACT) while satisfying heterogeneous resource constraints. Further, heterogeneous resource managers are tailored to efficiently support the action-level execution on resources with heterogeneous characteristics and topologies. Evaluation on real-world agentic RL tasks demonstrates that ARL-Tangram improves average ACT by up to 4.3$\times$, speeds up the step duration of RL training by up to 1.5$\times$, and saves the external resources by up to 71.2$\%$. This system has been deployed to support the training of the MiMo series models.

</details>


### [122] [A common parallel framework for LLP combinatorial problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13147)
*David Ribeiro Alves,Vijay K. Garg*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 提出了一个通用的无锁并行运行时LLP-FW，能够自动解决所有可表述为Lattice-Linear Predicate的组合优化问题，无需编写问题特定的同步代码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的无锁并行算法（如最短路径、稳定匹配、作业调度）需要程序员编写问题特定的代码和复杂的同步逻辑，这增加了开发难度和出错风险。

Method: 提出LLP-FW运行时，通过并行推进所有禁止的局部状态直到解出现，来解决可表述为Lattice-Linear Predicate的组合优化问题。程序员只需提供两个问题特定的定义：禁止状态检查和推进操作定义。

Result: LLP-FW成功应用于七种不同的组合优化问题：单源最短路径(SSSP)、广度优先搜索(BFS)、稳定婚姻、作业调度、传递闭包、并行归约和0-1背包问题。与手工调优的定制解决方案相比，在大多数情况下性能表现良好。

Conclusion: LLP-FW证明了一个通用无锁运行时可以有效解决多种组合优化问题，且性能可与手工优化的专用算法相媲美，为并行算法开发提供了新的通用框架。

Abstract: Traditional lock-free parallel algorithms for combinatorial optimization problems, such as shortest paths, stable matching, and job scheduling require programmers to write problem-specific routines and synchronization code. We propose a general-purpose lock-free runtime, LLP-FW that can solve all combinatorial optimization problems that can be formulated as a Lattice-Linear Predicate by advancing all forbidden local states in parallel until a solution emerges. The only problem-specific code is a definition of the forbiddenness check and a definition of the advancement. We show that LLP-FW can solve several different combinatorial optimization problems, such as Single Source Shortest Paths (SSSP), Breadth-First Search (BFS), Stable Marriage, Job Scheduling, Transitive Closure, Parallel Reduction, and 0-1 Knapsack. We compare LLP-FW against hand-tuned, custom solutions for these seven problems and show that it compares favorably in the majority of cases.

</details>

### [123] [DIALECTIC: A Multi-Agent System for Startup Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12274)
*Jae Yoon Bae,Simon Malberg,Joyce Galang,Andre Retterath,Georg Groh*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出了DIALECTIC，一个基于大语言模型（LLM）的多智能体系统，旨在通过模拟辩论的方式辅助风险投资（VC）投资者评估初创企业，其预测成功率已达到人类VC投资者的精度水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 风险投资投资者面临大量投资机会，但仅能投资少数项目，且最终成功的项目更少。由于投资者精力有限，早期筛选机会时必须在评估严谨度和评估数量之间进行权衡，亟需一种工具来缓解这一矛盾。

Method: 提出DIALECTIC系统，首先收集初创企业的事实知识并将其组织成分层问题树；然后将事实合成为支持与反对投资的自然语言论据，通过模拟辩论的方式迭代批评和修正这些论据，筛选出最具说服力的论据；系统还生成数值决策分数，帮助投资者对机会进行排序和优先级划分。

Result: 通过在五个VC基金汇总的真实投资机会上进行回测评估，结果显示DIALECTIC在预测初创企业成功率方面的精度与人类VC投资者相当。

Conclusion: DIALECTIC能够有效辅助风险投资投资者进行早期项目筛选，在保持预测精度的同时提高评估效率，缓解了投资者在评估严谨度和数量之间的权衡问题。

Abstract: Venture capital (VC) investors face a large number of investment opportunities but only invest in few of these, with even fewer ending up successful. Early-stage screening of opportunities is often limited by investor bandwidth, demanding tradeoffs between evaluation diligence and number of opportunities assessed. To ease this tradeoff, we introduce DIALECTIC, an LLM-based multi-agent system for startup evaluation. DIALECTIC first gathers factual knowledge about a startup and organizes these facts into a hierarchical question tree. It then synthesizes the facts into natural-language arguments for and against an investment and iteratively critiques and refines these arguments through a simulated debate, which surfaces only the most convincing arguments. Our system also produces numeric decision scores that allow investors to rank and thus efficiently prioritize opportunities. We evaluate DIALECTIC through backtesting on real investment opportunities aggregated from five VC funds, showing that DIALECTIC matches the precision of human VCs in predicting startup success.

</details>


### [124] [Collaborative Multi-Agent Optimization for Personalized Memory System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.12631)
*Wenyu Mao,Haoyang Liu,Zhao Liu,Haosong Tan,Yaorui Shi,Jiancan Wu,An Zhang,Xiang Wang*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出了CoMAM框架，通过协同强化学习联合优化多智能体记忆系统中的各个智能体，解决现有方法独立优化局部智能体而忽视智能体间协作的问题，从而提升个性化大语言模型的全局系统性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有面向个性化大语言模型的记忆系统通常采用多智能体架构来处理多粒度记忆构建与个性化记忆检索任务，但现有方法主要通过提示工程或微调独立优化各局部智能体，忽视了智能体间的协作，导致局部优化难以保证全局系统性能。

Method: 提出面向多智能体记忆系统的协同强化学习框架（CoMAM）。具体方法包括：(1)将智能体执行过程建模为序贯马尔可夫决策过程（MDP），将智能体间依赖关系嵌入状态转移，同时设计局部任务奖励（如记忆构建的信息覆盖率）和全局奖励（如问答准确率）；(2)通过局部奖励与全局奖励之间的组级排序一致性量化各智能体的贡献，将其作为自适应权重分配全局信用并融合局部-全局奖励；(3)各智能体基于融合奖励进行优化，实现局部改进与全局性能的对齐。

Result: 实验结果表明，CoMAM框架在多项任务上优于当前领先的记忆系统，验证了协同强化学习进行联合优化的有效性。

Conclusion: 通过协同强化学习框架联合优化多智能体记忆系统，能够有效促进智能体间协作，实现局部优化与全局性能的对齐，显著提升个性化大语言模型记忆系统的整体表现。

Abstract: Memory systems are crucial to personalized LLMs by mitigating the context window limitation in capturing long-term user-LLM conversations. Typically, such systems leverage multiple agents to handle multi-granular memory construction and personalized memory retrieval tasks. To optimize the system, existing methods focus on specializing agents on their local tasks independently via prompt engineering or fine-tuning. However, they overlook cross-agent collaboration, where independent optimization on local agents hardly guarantees the global system performance. To address this issue, we propose a Collaborative Reinforcement Learning Framework for Multi-Agent Memory Systems (CoMAM), jointly optimizing local agents to facilitate collaboration. Specifically, we regularize agents' execution as a sequential Markov decision process (MDP) to embed inter-agent dependencies into the state transition, yielding both local task rewards (e.g., information coverage for memory construction) and global rewards (i.e., query-answer accuracy). Then, we quantify each agent's contribution via group-level ranking consistency between local and global rewards, treating them as adaptive weights to assign global credit and integrate local-global rewards. Each agent is optimized by these integrated rewards, aligning local improvements with the global performance. Experiments show CoMAM outperforms leading memory systems, validating the efficacy of our proposed collaborative reinforcement learning for joint optimization.

</details>


### [125] [LLM Constitutional Multi-Agent Governance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13189)
*J. de Curtò,I. de Zarzà*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出宪法多智能体治理框架（CMAG）和伦理合作评分（ECS），在LLM驱动的多智能体系统中平衡合作收益与伦理风险，证明无约束优化虽提高合作率但严重侵蚀自治与公平性，而CMAG能在保持高自治（0.985）与诚信（0.995）的同时实现14.9%的伦理评分提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型能够生成有说服力的影响策略以促进多智能体群体合作，但关键问题在于：这种合作是否反映了真正的亲社会一致性，还是掩盖了智能体自治权、认知完整性和分配公平性的侵蚀？现有研究缺乏对LLM中介影响的伦理约束机制。

Method: 提出宪法多智能体治理（CMAG）两阶段框架，在LLM策略编译器和网络化智能体群体之间介入，结合硬约束过滤与软惩罚效用优化，平衡合作潜力与操纵风险及自治压力。引入伦理合作评分（ECS），通过合作、自治、诚信和公平的乘法组合来惩罚通过操纵手段达成的合作。在80个智能体的无标度网络上进行对抗条件（70%违规候选者）实验，对比全CMAG、朴素过滤和无约束优化三种机制。

Result: 无约束优化实现最高原始合作率（0.873），但由于严重的自治侵蚀（0.867）和公平性下降（0.888），ECS最低（0.645）。CMAG的ECS为0.741（提升14.9%），同时保持自治0.985、诚信0.995，合作率仅小幅降至0.770。朴素消融实验（ECS=0.733）证明单纯硬约束不足。帕累托分析显示CMAG主导合作-自治权衡空间，治理措施将枢纽-边缘暴露差异降低60%以上。

Conclusion: 合作若无治理并非本质上可取：宪法约束对于确保LLM中介影响产生伦理稳定结果而非操纵均衡是必要的。CMAG框架成功证明了在维持高伦理标准的同时实现有效合作的可行性。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) can generate persuasive influence strategies that shift cooperative behavior in multi-agent populations, but a critical question remains: does the resulting cooperation reflect genuine prosocial alignment, or does it mask erosion of agent autonomy, epistemic integrity, and distributional fairness? We introduce Constitutional Multi-Agent Governance (CMAG), a two-stage framework that interposes between an LLM policy compiler and a networked agent population, combining hard constraint filtering with soft penalized-utility optimization that balances cooperation potential against manipulation risk and autonomy pressure. We propose the Ethical Cooperation Score (ECS), a multiplicative composite of cooperation, autonomy, integrity, and fairness that penalizes cooperation achieved through manipulative means. In experiments on scale-free networks of 80 agents under adversarial conditions (70% violating candidates), we benchmark three regimes: full CMAG, naive filtering, and unconstrained optimization. While unconstrained optimization achieves the highest raw cooperation (0.873), it yields the lowest ECS (0.645) due to severe autonomy erosion (0.867) and fairness degradation (0.888). CMAG attains an ECS of 0.741, a 14.9% improvement, while preserving autonomy at 0.985 and integrity at 0.995, with only modest cooperation reduction to 0.770. The naive ablation (ECS = 0.733) confirms that hard constraints alone are insufficient. Pareto analysis shows CMAG dominates the cooperation-autonomy trade-off space, and governance reduces hub-periphery exposure disparities by over 60%. These findings establish that cooperation is not inherently desirable without governance: constitutional constraints are necessary to ensure that LLM-mediated influence produces ethically stable outcomes rather than manipulative equilibria.

</details>


### [126] [A Generative Model of Conspicuous Consumption and Status Signaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.13220)
*Logan Cross,Jordi Grau-Moya,William A. Cunningham,Alexander Sasha Vezhnevets,Joel Z. Leibo*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于“适当性理论”的地位计算理论，通过LLM智能体仿真验证了地位符号经由社会观察和预测模式补全的反馈循环内生涌现，揭示了社会互动如何将功能需求转化为地位寻求行为及文化规范的动态形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典成本信号理论将偏好视为固定，难以解释特定商品、信号或行为如何获得声望、符号意义如何随情境变化或随时间动态漂移甚至达到临界点，缺乏对地位符号生成机制的动态解释。

Method: 提出基于适当性理论的地位计算模型，在Concordia框架中使用大语言模型（LLM）智能体群体仿真，通过实验操控社会可见性模拟自然主义智能体日常互动，研究地位符号的内生涌现机制。

Result: 社会互动将功能需求转化为地位寻求行为，奢侈品和合成商品出现价格上涨和正价格弹性（凡勃伦效应），排除预训练偏差作为唯一驱动因素；"影响者"智能体通过定向制裁驱动亚文化内生形成，社会影响效应推广至非货币信号行为。

Conclusion: 本研究在微观认知与宏观经济、社会学现象之间建立了生成性桥梁，提供了一种预测文化规范如何从互动中涌现的新方法论，揭示了地位符号动态演化的内生机制。

Abstract: Status signaling drives human behavior and the allocation of scarce resources such as mating opportunities, yet the generative mechanisms governing how specific goods, signals, or behaviors acquire prestige remain a puzzle. Classical frameworks, such as Costly Signaling Theory, treat preferences as fixed and struggle to explain how semiotic meaning changes based on context or drifts dynamically over time, occasionally reaching tipping points. In this work, we propose a computational theory of status grounded in the theory of appropriateness, positing that status symbols emerge endogenously through a feedback loop of social observation and predictive pattern completion. We validate this theory using simulations of groups of Large Language Model (LLM)-based agents in the Concordia framework. By experimentally manipulating social visibility within naturalistic agent daily routines, we demonstrate that social interactions transform functional demand into status-seeking behavior. We observe the emergence of price run-ups and positive price elasticity (Veblen effects) for both real-world luxury items and procedurally generated synthetic goods, ruling out pretraining bias as the sole driver. Furthermore, we demonstrate that "influencer" agents can drive the endogenous formation of distinct subcultures through targeted sanctioning, and find that similar social influence effects generalize to non-monetary signaling behaviors. This work provides a generative bridge between micro-level cognition and macro-level economic and sociological phenomena, offering a new methodology for forecasting how cultural conventions emerge from interaction.

</details>
